<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 2.02&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Results of Operations and Financial Condition</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On January&nbsp;17, 2007,
Apple&nbsp;Inc. (&#147;Apple&#148;) issued a press release regarding Apple&#146;s preliminary
financial results for its first fiscal quarter ended December&nbsp;30, 2006 and
a related data sheet. A copy of Apple&#146;s press release is attached hereto as
Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 and a copy of the related data sheet is attached hereto as
Exhibit&nbsp;99.2.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The information contained
in this Current Report shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for purposes of
Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#147;Exchange
Act&#148;), or incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of
1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth
by specific reference in such a filing.</font></p>

<body lang="EN-US">

<div>

<p align="right" style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple Reports First Quarter Results</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Revenue Exceeds $7 Billion; Record Profit of $1
Billion</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">CUPERTINO, California&#151;January 17, 2007&#151;Apple&#174; today
announced financial results for its fiscal 2007 first quarter ended December
30, 2006. The Company posted record revenue of $7.1 billion and record net
quarterly profit of $1.0 billion, or $1.14 per diluted share. These results
compare to revenue of $5.7 billion and net quarterly profit of $565 million, or
$.65 per diluted share, in the year-ago quarter. Gross margin was 31.2 percent,
up from 27.2 percent in the year-ago quarter. International sales accounted for
42 percent of the quarter&#146;s revenue.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple shipped 1,606,000 Macintosh&#174; computers and
21,066,000 iPods during the quarter, representing 28 percent growth in Macs and
50 percent growth in iPods over the year-ago quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We are incredibly pleased to report record quarterly
revenue of over $7 billion and record earnings of $1 billion,&#148; said Steve Jobs,
Apple&#146;s CEO. &#147;We&#146;ve just kicked off what is going to be a very strong new
product year for Apple by launching Apple TV and the revolutionary iPhone.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We generated over $1.75 billion in cash during the
quarter to end with $11.9 billion,&#148; said Peter Oppenheimer, Apple&#146;s CFO. &#147;Looking
ahead to the second fiscal quarter of 2007, we expect revenue of $4.8 to $4.9
billion and earnings per diluted share of $.54 to $.56.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple will provide live streaming of its Q1 2007
financial results conference call utilizing QuickTime&#174;, Apple&#146;s standards-based
technology for live and on-demand audio and video streaming. The live webcast
will begin at 2:00 p.m. PST on Wednesday, January 17, 2007 at
www.apple.com/quicktime/qtv/earningsq107/ and will also be available for
replay. The QuickTime player is available free for Macintosh and Windows users
at www.apple.com/quicktime.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">-more-</font></p>

<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\fc\1703945735_D11154_1615066\1998-1-mm.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Jan 17 00:39 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press release contains forward-looking statements
about the Company&#146;s estimated revenue and earnings per share. These statements
involve risks and uncertainties, and actual results may differ. Risks and
uncertainties include potential litigation and government enforcement actions
that may result from the matters investigated by the special committee of the
board of directors and the restatement of the Company&#146;s consolidated financial
statements; unfavorable results of legal proceedings; the effect of competitive
and economic factors, and the Company&#146;s reaction to those factors, on consumer
and business buying decisions with respect to the Company&#146;s products; war,
terrorism, public health issues, and other circumstances that could disrupt
supply, delivery, or demand of products; continued competitive pressures in the
marketplace;&#160; the continued availability
on acceptable terms of certain components and services essential to the Company&#146;s
business currently obtained by the Company from sole or limited sources; the
ability of the Company to make timely delivery of new programs, products and
successful technological innovations to the marketplace; the effect that
product quality problems could have on the Company&#146;s sales and operating
profits; the inventory risk associated with the Company&#146;s need to order or
commit to order product components in advance of customer orders; the effect
that the Company&#146;s dependency on manufacturing and logistics services provided
by third parties may have on the quality, quantity or cost of products
manufactured or services rendered; the Company&#146;s dependency on the performance
of distributors and other resellers of the Company&#146;s products; the Company&#146;s
reliance on the availability of third-party digital content; the potential
impact of a finding that the Company has infringed on the intellectual property
rights of others; and risks associated with the Company&#146;s retail initiative,
including significant investment cost, uncertain consumer acceptance and
potential impact on existing reseller relationships. More information on
potential factors that could affect the Company&#146;s financial results is included
from time to time in the Company&#146;s public reports filed with the SEC, including
the Company&#146;s Form 10-K for the fiscal year ended September 30, 2006 and the
Company&#146;s Form 10-Q for the quarter ended December 30, 2006 to be filed with
the SEC. The Company assumes no obligation to update any forward-looking
statements or information, which speak as of their respective dates.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Apple
ignited the personal computer revolution in the 1970s with the Apple II and
reinvented the personal computer in the 1980s with the Macintosh. Today, Apple
continues to lead the industry in innovation with its award-winning desktop and
notebook computers, OS X operating system, and iLife and professional
applications. Apple is also spearheading the digital music revolution with its
iPod portable music players and iTunes online store.</font></p>
